<script>
function DoAuth()
{
    //先写用户状态，通知STB
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UserStatus','0');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('PlatformCode','0102');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('EncryptionType','0001');

    document.authform.Lang.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("Lang");
    document.authform.SupportHD.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("SupportHD");
    document.authform.NetUserID.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("NetUserID");
    document.authform.UserID.value = "1574120801251245";
    var stbType = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("STBType");

    //判断(机顶盒型号 == 华为的盒子型号)，则重置加密方式为DES，密码为111111
    if (stbType == "EC1308B_pub" || stbType == "EC2108" || stbType == "EC5108G_pub")
    {
        //调用盒子接口设置加密方式为DES
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig("EncryptionType","0001");

        //调用盒子接口设置密码=111111
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig("Pwd","111111");

    }

    var stbType= Authentication.CTCGetConfig("STBType");
    document.authform.STBType.value = stbType;
    document.authform.STBVersion.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("STBVersion");
    document.authform.SoftwareVersion.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("SoftwareVersion");
    document.authform.IsSmartStb.value = 0;
    document.authform.desktopId.value = Utility.getValueByName('TVDesktopID');
    document.authform.conntype.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("ConnectType");

    document.authform.templateName.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("templateName");
    document.authform.areaId.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("areaid");
    document.authform.userGroupId.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("UserGroupNMB");
    document.authform.productPackageId.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("PackageIDs");
    document.authform.UserField.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("UserField");
    
    getSTBAuthenticator();
    
    document.authform.submit();
}

function getSTBAuthenticator()
{
    document.authform.STBID.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("STBID");   
    var EncryptToken = "39D0C1C0EBC8EA5625C5EE49652D836B";
    document.authform.Authenticator.value = Authentication.CTCGetAuthInfo(EncryptToken);
    document.authform.userToken.value = "39D0C1C0EBC8EA5625C5EE49652D836B";
    document.authform.mac.value = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("mac");
}

</script>

<script language="javascript">
/* java变量与js 变量转换*/
var isSucessed = true;
var isWriteBox = true;
var needWriteTSP = true;
function AuthFinish()
{
    /* 认证成功才写入 */
    var tempKey = "";
    if (isSucessed)
    {
        if (false)
        {
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('Tools.Record.AddRecord','{"key":"X_CSRFToken","value":"null","type":"1"}');
        }
        if (false)
        {
            Utility.setValueByName('authStatus','{"status":"1","errorCode":"","errorType":"","errorName":"","errorDesc":"","errorResolve":""}');
            Utility.setValueByName('TVDesktopID','');
            Utility.setValueByName('TVDesktopGetURL','');
            // 智能机顶盒容灾情况下也下发UserToken，否则无法获取桌面数据
            if (!isWriteBox)
            {
                Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UserToken','BIiy2BIiy26YRQXULJgbHL8i4XpsF3sN');               
            }
        }
         
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('IsPostLog','0');   
        
        setStbParmList();
        
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('SQARtcpPort','8027');
        if("1" == '1')
        {
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('user_type','1');
        }

        /* 容灾状态这些值没必要再下发给盒子了*/
        if (isWriteBox)  
        {
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UserToken','BIiy2BIiy26YRQXULJgbHL8i4XpsF3sN');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('EPGDomain','http://218.71.130.67:33200/EPG/jsp/epg30/en/Category.jsp');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('EPGDomainBackup','null');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('ManagementDomain','http://stb.zj.vnet.cn:37021/acs');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('ManagementDomainBackup','null');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UpgradeDomain','http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UpgradeDomainBackup',' ');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('NTPDomain','122.229.6.55');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('NTPDomainBackup','122.229.6.56');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('EPGGroupNMB','epg30');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UserGroupNMB','12');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('PackageIDs','');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('subNetId','8601');
            
            if (true)
            {
                if (false)
                {
                    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('NetUserID','tv1574120801251245@itv');
                }
            }
            
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('areaid','303');
            Authentication.CTCSetConfig('templateName','epg30');
        }

        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('shareKey','null');
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('LogServerUrl','sftp://username:password@IP:port/path');
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('LogUploadInterval','3600');
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('LogRecordInterval','3600');
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('EPGUrl','http://218.71.130.67:33200/EPG/jsp/indexHWCTC.jsp');
        
        //写用户认证通过标志
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UserStatus','1');
        
        if (needWriteTSP)
        {
           Authentication.CTCSetConfig('TransportProtocol','0');
        }
        
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('MQMCURL','122.229.6.226');
        //认证成功后,非空的PPPoE才写入机顶盒. 只能放在最后写入,详见问题单

        setSTBConfig();
        
        Authentication.CTCSetConfig('SessionID','02RFFX6CR2DQ42ERBS0AM8O13JY0TPFJ');

        tempKey = Authentication.CTCGetConfig('identityEncode');
        document.authform.tempKey.value = tempKey;
    }

    document.authform.submit();
}

function setSTBConfig()
{
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('UserID','1574120801251245');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('TVMSHeartbitUrl','http://www.TVMSHeartbitUrl.com');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('TVMSVODHeartbitUrl','http://www.TVMSVODHeartbitUrl.com');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('TVMSHeartbitInterval','600');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('TVMSDelayLength','60');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig("ResServerUrl", "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234" + "/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp");
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('ADPlatformUrl','http://122.229.17.132:9091/adsserver/web/adreq');
    Authentication.CTCSetConfig('AuthenBackgroundPicTime','10');
    setBootPic();
    
    Authentication.CTCStartUpdate();    
}

function getUrlParameter(url, paramtername)
{
	 var name = paramtername +"=";
	 var value =url.substring(url.indexOf(name) + name.length);
	 if (value.indexOf("&") != -1){
		 value =value.substring(0, value.indexOf("&"));
	 }
	 //console.log(paramtername +"= " +value);
	return value;
}

function setBootPic()
{
    //下发开机画面
    var bootLogo = "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=0&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1";     
    var authenBack = "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=1&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1";
    var bootLoad = "null";
	var bootAny = "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=3&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1";
    var bootLogo_old = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("PADBootLogPicURL");
    var authenBack_old = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("PADAuthenBackgroundPicURL");
    var bootLoad_old = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("PADLoaderLogoPicURL");
	var bootAny_old = Authentication.CTCGetConfig("BootanimationURL");
    var isSupportAD = "0";
    
    //对接广告平台时
    if (1 == isSupportAD)
    {
        if (bootLogo != '' && bootLogo != 'null')
        {
            if (bootLogo != bootLogo_old)
            {
                Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADBootLogPicURL", bootLogo);  
            }
        }
        if (authenBack != '' && authenBack != 'null' && ("1" == '1'))
        {
            if (authenBack != authenBack_old)
            {
                Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADAuthenBackgroundPicURL", authenBack);   
            }
        }
    }
    //个性化开机画面流程
    else
    {
     
        		 var sJson= Authentication.CTCGetConfig('commonInfo, {"type":"bootPic"}');
        		 if (sJson.downLoadURL != "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=5&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1")
        		 {
        		     Authentication.CTCSetConfig('commonInfo','{"type":"bootPic","downLoadURL":"http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=5&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1","infoDesc":""}');
        		 }
            
        		 var sJson= Authentication.CTCGetConfig('commonInfo, {"type":"fastPlay"}');
        		 if (sJson.downLoadURL != "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=6&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1")
        		 {
        		     Authentication.CTCSetConfig('commonInfo','{"type":"fastPlay","downLoadURL":"http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=6&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1","infoDesc":""}');
        		 }
            
        		 var sJson= Authentication.CTCGetConfig('commonInfo, {"type":"bootanimation"}');
        		 if (sJson.downLoadURL != "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=7&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1")
        		 {
        		     Authentication.CTCSetConfig('commonInfo','{"type":"bootanimation","downLoadURL":"http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=7&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1","infoDesc":""}');
        		 }
            
        		 var sJson= Authentication.CTCGetConfig('commonInfo, {"type":"authPic"}');
        		 if (sJson.downLoadURL != "http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=8&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1")
        		 {
        		     Authentication.CTCSetConfig('commonInfo','{"type":"authPic","downLoadURL":"http://www.qeweryeryy.com:1234/EDS/jsp/loadBootpic.jsp?STBType=HG680-JD4EH-52&areaid=57&PicType=8&userId=1574120801251245&userGroupId=12&isIndiv=1","infoDesc":""}');
        		 }
            

        if (bootLogo != '' && bootLogo != 'null')
        {
            if (-1 == bootLogo.indexOf("FILENAME=") || undefined == bootLogo_old || -1 == bootLogo_old.indexOf("FILENAME="))
            {
                //如果不带FILENAME字段说明EPG没有匹配到策略，这时再发请求在UPG端再进行匹配
                Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADBootLogPicURL", bootLogo);  
            }
            else
            {
                //截取出filename进行比较
                var bootLogo_filename = getUrlParameter(bootLogo, "FILENAME");
                var bootLogo_old_filename = getUrlParameter(bootLogo_old, "FILENAME");
                if (bootLogo_filename != bootLogo_old_filename)
                {
                    Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADBootLogPicURL", bootLogo);  
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (authenBack != '' && authenBack != 'null' && ("1" == '1'))
        {
            if (-1 == authenBack.indexOf("FILENAME=") || undefined == authenBack_old || -1 == authenBack_old.indexOf("FILENAME="))
            {
                Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADAuthenBackgroundPicURL", authenBack);   
            }
            else
            {
                //截取出filename进行比较 
                var authenBack_filename = getUrlParameter(authenBack, "FILENAME");
                var authenBack_old_filename = getUrlParameter(authenBack_old, "FILENAME");
                if (authenBack_filename != authenBack_old_filename)
                {
                    Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADAuthenBackgroundPicURL", authenBack);   
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (bootLoad != '' && bootLoad != 'null')
        {
            if (-1 == bootLoad.indexOf("FILENAME=") || undefined == bootLoad_old ||  -1 == bootLoad_old.indexOf("FILENAME="))
            {
                Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADLoaderLogoPicURL", bootLoad);   
            }
            else
            {
                //截取出filename进行比较
                var bootLoad_filename = getUrlParameter(bootLoad, "FILENAME");
                var bootLoad_old_filename = getUrlParameter(bootLoad_old, "FILENAME");
                if (bootLoad_filename != bootLoad_old_filename)
                {
                    Authentication.CTCSetConfig("PADLoaderLogoPicURL", bootLoad);
                }
            }
        }
		
        if (bootAny != '' && bootAny != 'null')
        {
            if (-1 == bootAny.indexOf("FILENAME=") || undefined == bootAny_old ||  -1 == bootAny_old.indexOf("FILENAME="))
            {
                Authentication.CTCSetConfig("BootanimationURL", bootAny);
            }
            else
            {
                //截取出filename进行比较
                var bootAny_filename = getUrlParameter(bootAny, "FILENAME");
                var bootAny_old_filename = getUrlParameter(bootAny_old, "FILENAME");
                if (bootAny_filename != bootAny_old_filename)
                {
                    Authentication.CTCSetConfig("BootanimationURL", bootAny);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

{

    var targetUrl = '';

        var isGoChannel = false;
        if (isGoChannel)
        {

	if ((typeof Authentication) != "undefined") {
		return Authentication.CTCGetConfig(name);
	} else {
		return "";
	}

try{
	var STB = navigator.appName;
	if(STB == "Ranger" || STB == "EIS iPanel"){//机顶盒浏览器区分 华为 创维
		iPanel.focusWidth = "-10";//焦点框宽度
	}else if(STB == "ztebw" || STB.indexOf("Fhbw")>=0){//中兴 烽火
		iPanel.focusWidth = "0";//焦点框宽度
	}else{
		iPanel.focusWidth = "-1";//焦点框宽度
	}
}catch(e){
	iPanel.focusWidth = "-1";//焦点框宽度

function $(id) {
    if (document.getElementById(id)) {
        return document.getElementById(id);
    } else if (document.all) {
        return document.all[id];
    }
}

var commonTools = {
	bgColor : "#272d2e",
	pxGet : function(num) {//720P跟1080P的显示倍数
		var MPL = document.querySelector('meta[name=page-view-size]').content == "1920*1080" ? 1.5 : 1;
		num = Math.round(num*MPL);
		return num;
	},
	resolution : function() {//探针720P跟1080P拼接名字
		var name = document.querySelector('meta[name=page-view-size]').content == "1920*1080" ? "1080" : "720";
		return name;
	},
	docCreate : function(elType,attList){
		var newEl = document.createElement(elType);
		var newAtt = "", getAtt = "", attStr = "";
		for(var i=0; i<attList.length; i++){
			getAtt = attList[i].split("|");
			attStr = "";
			if (getAtt[0] == "style" && (getAtt[1].indexOf("top") != -1 || getAtt[1].indexOf("left") != -1 || getAtt[1].indexOf("width") != -1 || getAtt[1].indexOf("height") != -1)) {
				var dataArray = getAtt[1].split(";");
				var dataArray = dataArray.filter(function (s) {
				   return s && commonTools.trim(s);
				});

				for (var j = 0; j < dataArray.length; j++) {
					var pxNum = 0;
					if (dataArray[j].indexOf("top") != -1) {
						attStr += "top:"+commonTools.pxGet(parseInt(commonTools.deletePx(commonTools.getValueByKey(dataArray, "top")),10))+"px;";
					} else if (dataArray[j].indexOf("left") != -1) {
						attStr += "left:"+commonTools.pxGet(parseInt(commonTools.deletePx(commonTools.getValueByKey(dataArray, "left")),10))+"px;";
					} else if (dataArray[j].indexOf("width") != -1) {
						attStr += "width:"+commonTools.pxGet(parseInt(commonTools.deletePx(commonTools.getValueByKey(dataArray, "width")),10))+"px;";
					} else if (dataArray[j].indexOf("line-height") != -1) {
						attStr += "line-height:"+commonTools.pxGet(parseInt(commonTools.deletePx(commonTools.getValueByKey(dataArray, "line-height")),10))+"px;";
					} else if (dataArray[j].indexOf("height") != -1) {
						attStr += "height:"+commonTools.pxGet(parseInt(commonTools.deletePx(commonTools.getValueByKey(dataArray, "height")),10))+"px;";
					} else if (dataArray[j].indexOf("font-size") != -1) {
						attStr += "font-size:"+commonTools.pxGet(parseInt(commonTools.deletePx(commonTools.getValueByKey(dataArray, "font-size")),10))+"px;";
					} else {
						attStr += dataArray[j]+";";
					}
				}
			} else if (elType == "img" && (getAtt[0] == "width" || getAtt[0] == "height")) {
				attStr = commonTools.pxGet(parseInt(getAtt[1],10));
			} else {
				attStr = getAtt[1];
			}

			newAtt = document.createAttribute(getAtt[0]);
			newAtt.nodeValue = attStr;
			newEl.setAttributeNode(newAtt);
		}
		return newEl;
	},
	txtCreate : function(txtList){
		txtList = txtList.toString();
		var txtVal = "";
		for(var i=0; i<txtList.length; i++){
			if(txtList[i] != null && txtList[i] != "null" && txtList[i] != ""){
				txtVal += txtList[i];
			}
		}
		return document.createTextNode(txtVal);
	},
	debug : function(val){
		if(!$("debugTest")){
			var testDiv = this.docCreate("div",["id|debugTest","style|position:absolute; overflow:hidden; word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; left:30px; top:30px; width:1220px; height:680px; background-color:#001; opacity:0.5; line-height:24px; color:#FFF; font-size:20px; z-index:999;"]);
			document.body.appendChild(testDiv);
		}
		if (typeof(val) == "object") {
			val = JSON.stringify(val);
		}
		$("debugTest").innerText = commonDate.dateFormat("yyyy年MM月dd日 hh:mm:ss:S")+" : "+val+"\n"+$("debugTest").innerText;
	},
	zeroPad : function(num, n) {//字符串前面补零 ，num参数，n总位数
	    var len = num.toString().length;
	    while(len < n) {
	        num = "0" + num;
	        len++;
	    }
	    return num;
	},
	deletePx : function(_paramenter){//删除单位px并返回
		if(_paramenter.indexOf("px")>0){
			return parseInt(_paramenter.substring(0,_paramenter.length-2));
		}else{
			return parseInt(_paramenter);
		}
	},
	marqueeFocus : function(id, len){//字符串过长游走
		var yx_text = $(id).innerHTML;
		var dateLength = commonTools.DataLength(yx_text);
		if(dateLength > len){
			$(id).innerHTML = "<marquee scrollamount='5'>"+yx_text+"</marquee>";
		}
	},
	removeElement : function(_id){//根据id删除当前节点
        var _element = document.getElementById(_id);
        var _parentElement = _element.parentNode;
        if(_parentElement){
            _parentElement.removeChild(_element);
        }
    },
	DataLength : function(fData){//fData字符串，返回字符串长度
		fData = fData.toString();
	    var intLength=0
		for (var i=0; i<fData.length; i++){
			if ((fData.charCodeAt(i) < 0) || (fData.charCodeAt(i) > 255)){
				intLength = intLength+2;
			}else{
				intLength = intLength+1;
			}
		}
		return intLength;
	},
	DataLengthSub : function(fData, len){//字符串截取，fData字符串，len截取长度），返回截取后的字符串
		fData = fData.toString();
	    var intLength=0
		var tempStr = fData;
		if(commonTools.DataLength(fData) > len){
			for (var i=0; i<fData.length; i++){
				if ((fData.charCodeAt(i) < 0) || (fData.charCodeAt(i) > 255)){
					intLength = intLength+2;
				}else{
					intLength = intLength+1;
				}
				if(intLength >= len){
					tempStr = tempStr.slice(0,(i + 1))+"...";
					break;
			   }
			}
		}
		return tempStr;
	},
	deleName : function(vodName){/**去除资产名中的 HD- -HD HD 4K- -4K _4K 4K，替换中文_成英文_*/
		var newName = '';
		if(vodName.length > 0){
			newName = vodName.replace('HD-','').replace('-HD','').replace('HD','').replace('4K-','').replace('-4K','').replace('_4K','').replace('4K','');
            if (newName.indexOf("＿") != -1) { // 替换中文＿成英文_
                newName = newName.replace(/＿/g,"_");
            }
		}
		return newName;
	},
    isVIPEx : function (showFlag) {/**判断媒资是否收费,返回true、false,成思后台配置0001免费,0002为收费*/
        if (showFlag == '0002') {
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    },
	isVIP : function(code){/**判断媒资是否收费,成思后台配置0001免费,0002为收费*/
		var imgUrl = 'imgs/system/dot.gif';
		if (parseInt(code,10) > 100) {
			var width102 = ["0104","0105","0202","0204","0110","0111","0208","0209","0210","0211","0212"];
			if (width102.indexOf(code) != -1) {
				imgUrl = system_path_720+"Ver.2/imgs/superscript/"+code+"_102.png";
			} else {
				imgUrl = system_path_720+"Ver.2/imgs/superscript/"+code+"_54.png";
			}
		}
		return imgUrl;
	},
	strSubDate : function(vodName){
		var vodDate = "";
        var arr = vodName.match(/\d{7,}/g);
        if(arr != null && arr != "null" && arr != "") arr = arr.toString();
        if(arr.length == 8) vodDate = arr.substring(0,4)+"-"+arr.substring(4,6)+"-"+arr.substring(6,8);
        return vodDate;
	},
	getPageTotal : function(total,pageSize){//获取总页码
		var tempPageTotal = 1;
		if(total % pageSize == 0) tempPageTotal = Math.floor(total/pageSize);
		else tempPageTotal = Math.floor(total/pageSize)+1;
		tempPageTotal = tempPageTotal==0 ? 1:tempPageTotal;
		return tempPageTotal;
	},
	getPageCount : function(total,pageNo,pageSize){//获取每页数量
		var tempPageCount = 0;
		if(total/pageNo < pageSize) tempPageCount = total%pageSize;
		else tempPageCount = pageSize;
		return tempPageCount;
	},
    trim:function (str) { // 删除字符串左右两侧的空格
        return str.replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g,"");
    },
    protectPic : function(_id,_pic){//页面图片加载失败保护
        $(_id).childNodes[0].src = _pic;
	},
	addClass : function(_id, cls){
		var obj = $(_id);
		var obj_class = obj.className;//获取 class 内容.
		blank = (obj_class != '') ? ' ' : '';//判断获取到的 class 是否为空, 如果不为空在前面加个'空格'.
		added = obj_class + blank + cls;//组合原来的 class 和需要添加的 class.
		obj.className = added;//替换原来的 class.
	},
	removeClass : function(_id, cls){
		var obj = $(_id);
		var obj_class = ' '+obj.className+' ';//获取 class 内容, 并在首尾各加一个空格. ex) 'abc    bcd' -> ' abc    bcd '
		obj_class = obj_class.replace(/(\s+)/gi, ' '),//将多余的空字符替换成一个空格. ex) ' abc    bcd ' -> ' abc bcd '
		removed = obj_class.replace(' '+cls+' ', ' ');//在原来的 class 替换掉首尾加了空格的 class. ex) ' abc bcd ' -> 'bcd '
		removed = removed.replace(/(^\s+)|(\s+$)/g, '');//去掉首尾空格. ex) 'bcd ' -> 'bcd'
		obj.className = removed;//替换原来的 class.
	},
	hasClass : function(_id, cls){
		var obj = $(_id);
		var obj_class = obj.className;//获取 class 内容.
		obj_class_lst = obj_class.split(/\s+/);//通过split空字符将cls转换成数组.
		x = 0;
		for(x in obj_class_lst) {
		  if(obj_class_lst[x] == cls) {//循环数组, 判断是否包含cls
			return true;
		  }
		}
		return false;
	},
	getValueByKey:function(arr, key) {
		var returnStr = "";
        if (arr == null || arr.length == 0) {
            return returnStr;
        }
        
        var keyName, keyValue;
        for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
        	if (arr[i].indexOf("：") != -1) {
	        	keyName = arr[i].substring(0,arr[i].indexOf("："));
	            keyValue = arr[i].substring(arr[i].indexOf("：")+1,arr[i].length);
	        } else if (arr[i].indexOf(":") != -1) {
	            keyName = arr[i].substring(0,arr[i].indexOf(":"));
	            keyValue = arr[i].substring(arr[i].indexOf(":")+1,arr[i].length);
	        }
            if (commonTools.trim(keyName).toUpperCase() == key.toUpperCase()) {
                returnStr = keyValue;
                break;
            }
        }
        return returnStr;
    }
}

var commonAAA = {
	GDAAAFlag : true,			//双3A
	GDAAAGroupFlag : false,		//双3A分组判断
	GDAAAServer : 'http://115.233.200.94:58002/aaa/Service',//3A服务器地址：正式http://115.233.200.94:58002 测试http://115.233.200.102:58006
	GDAAASPID : 'zjxmt',		//3A中SP编码
	GDAAATimeFunction : 0,		//超时函数
	GDAAATime : 1000,			//超时时间
	auth : function(ajaxFun,userId,_type,mediaCode,callBackFunction){
    	commonAAA.GDAAATimeFunction = setTimeout(callBackFunction,commonAAA.GDAAATime);
		jsonpData({
			url: 'api/service/'+mediaCode+'.json',
			key: 'getJsonDate',
			data: {type:_type},
			callback: function(data){
				var dataJSON = data.resultSet;
				var ServiceCodes = '';
				for(var i=0; i<dataJSON.length; i++){
					ServiceCodes += dataJSON[i].code;
					if(i<dataJSON.length-1)ServiceCodes += ','
				}
				var _data = {
						"UserId" : userId,
						"SpId" : commonAAA.GDAAASPID,
						"UserToken" : commonCookie.getCookie("GDAAAUserToken"),
						"ServiceCodes" : ServiceCodes,
						"ContentCode" : mediaCode
				}
				var _url = commonAAA.GDAAAServer + "/Auth";
				ajaxFun.getAJAXData({
					url : _url,
					type : 'POST',
					data : JSON.stringify(_data),
					callback : function(data){
						clearTimeout(commonAAA.GDAAATimeFunction);
						callBackFunction(data);
					}
				});
			}
		});
	},
	order : function(ajaxFun,userId,productCode,callBackFunction){
		commonAAA.GDAAATimeFunction = setTimeout(callBackFunction,commonAAA.GDAAATime);
		var _data = {
				"UserId" : userId,
				"SpId" : "zjxmt",
				"UserToken" : commonCookie.getCookie("GDAAAUserToken"),
				"Action" : "1",
				"ProductCode" : productCode,
				"PayType" : "1"
			}
		var _url = commonAAA.GDAAAServer + "/Order";
		ajaxFun.getAJAXData({
			url : _url,
			type : 'POST',
			data : JSON.stringify(_data),
			callback : function(data){
				clearTimeout(commonAAA.GDAAATimeFunction);
				if(data.Result == '000' || data.Result == '3011'){
					commonCookie.setCookie("OrderNo",data.OrderNo);
					callBackFunction();
				}else{
					commonAAA.toErrorPage(data);
				}
			}
		});
	},
	getPayNotify : function(ajaxFun,_no,callBackFunction){//支付通知接口，电信订购成功后调用该接口同步订购数据到广电AAA
		var _data = {
				"OrderId" : _no,
				"PayResult" : '0',
				"Sign" : md5(_no+'$0$Chances_2018')
			}
		var _url = commonAAA.GDAAAServer + "/PayNotify";
		ajaxFun.getAJAXData({
			url : _url,
			type : 'POST',
			data : JSON.stringify(_data),
			callback : function(data){
				if (callBackFunction && typeof callBackFunction == "function") {
					callBackFunction(data);
				}
			}
		});
	},
	toErrorPage : function(data){
        window.location.href = system_path_720+"Ver.2/pageError.jsp?errorCode="+data.Result+'&productCode='+data.ProductCode;
    }
}

var commonCookie = {
	setCookie : function(name,value){
		var cookies = name+'='+encodeURIComponent(value);
		cookies += ';max-age='+(30*60*60*24);
		cookies += ';path=/';
		document.cookie = cookies;
	},
	getCookie : function(key){
		var returnArgs = "";
		try{
			if(document.cookie.indexOf(";") == -1) return '';
			var arr1 = document.cookie.split('; ');
			for(var i=0;i<arr1.length;i++){
				var arr2 = arr1[i].split('=');
				if(arr2[0] == key){
					returnArgs = decodeURIComponent(arr2[1]);
				}
			}
		}catch(e){
		}
		if(typeof(returnArgs) == "undefined"){
			return '';
		}else{
			return returnArgs;
		}
	}	
}

var commonDate = {
	timeFormat : function(seconds,format){//时间格式化，seconds秒，format格式，返回转换后时间格式
		var hour = commonTools.zeroPad(Math.floor(seconds/3600),2);
		var minute = commonTools.zeroPad(Math.floor(seconds/60-hour*60),2);
		var ss = commonTools.zeroPad(Math.floor(seconds-hour*3600-minute*60),2);
		return ""+hour+format+minute+format+ss;
	},
	dateFormat:function(fmt){
        var date = new Date();
        var o = {
            "M+" : date.getMonth()+1,                 //月份
            "d+" : date.getDate(),                    //日
            "h+" : date.getHours(),                   //小时
            "m+" : date.getMinutes(),                 //分
            "s+" : date.getSeconds(),                 //秒
            "q+" : Math.floor((date.getMonth()+3)/3), //季度
            "S"  : date.getMilliseconds()             //毫秒
        };
        if(/(y+)/.test(fmt))
            fmt=fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, (date.getFullYear()+"").substr(4 - RegExp.$1.length));
        for(var k in o)
            if(new RegExp("("+ k +")").test(fmt))
                fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, (RegExp.$1.length==1) ? (o[k]) : (("00"+ o[k]).substr((""+ o[k]).length)));
        return fmt;
    },
	getDateStr : function(AddDayCount){
		var dd = new Date();
    	dd.setDate(dd.getDate()+AddDayCount);//获取AddDayCount天后的日期
    	var y = dd.getFullYear();
    	var m = dd.getMonth()+1;//获取当前月份的日期
    	var d = dd.getDate();
    	var week = dd.getDay();
    	var str = "";
    	switch(week){
    		case 0:
    			str = "周日";
    		break;
    		case 1:
    			str = "周一";
    		break;
    		case 2:
    			str = "周二";
    		break;
    		case 3:
    			str = "周三";
    		break;
    		case 4:
    			str = "周四";
    		break;
    		case 5:
    			str = "周五";
    		break;
    		case 6:
    			str = "周六";
    		break;
    	}
    	return m+"/"+d+"&nbsp;"+str;
	},
	getBackDate : function(AddDayCount){
		var dd = new Date();
    	dd.setDate(dd.getDate()+AddDayCount);//获取AddDayCount天后的日期
    	var y = dd.getFullYear();
    	var m = dd.getMonth()+1;//获取当前月份的日期
    	var d = dd.getDate();
    	m = commonTools.zeroPad(m,2);
    	d = commonTools.zeroPad(d,2);
    	return ""+y+m+d;
	}
}

var AjaxData = function(levels){
	if(this instanceof AjaxData){
		this.levels = levels;
	}else{
		return new AjaxData(levels);
	}
}
AjaxData.prototype = {
	timer : 0,
	xmlHttp : null,
	objPool : [],
	getAJAXData : function(setting){
		this.xmlHttp = this.getInstance();
        var data = setting.data || null;
        var type = setting.type || "GET";
        var query = [];
        for(var key in data){
            query.push(key + '=' + encodeURIComponent(data[key]));
        }
        setting.url = setting.url || (this.levels+"common/data.jsp?" + query.join('&'));
        setting.callback = setting.callback || function(){};
        setting.error = setting.error || setting.callback;
        setting.async = setting.async || true;
        setting.duration = setting.duration || 1000*2;
        var self = this;
        var timeOut = false;
        this.timer = setTimeout(function() {
	    	timeOut = true;
	    	self.xmlHttp.abort();
		}, setting.duration);
	    this.xmlHttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
			if (timeOut) {
				clearTimeout(this.timer);
				setting.error("timeOut");
			} else {
				self.stateChanged(setting);
			}
	    };
		this.xmlHttp.open(type, setting.url, setting.async);
		if (type == "POST" || type == "post") {
			this.xmlHttp.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8'); 
		}
	    this.xmlHttp.send(data);
	},
	getInstance : function() {
	    for (var i = 0; i < this.objPool.length; i ++) {
	        if (this.objPool[i].readyState == 4 || this.objPool[i].readyState == 0) {
	            return this.objPool[i];
	        }
	    }
	    this.objPool[this.objPool.length] = this.createXMLHttpRequest();
	    return this.objPool[this.objPool.length - 1];
	},
	stateChanged : function(setting) {
	    if (this.xmlHttp.readyState == 4) {
	    	if (this.xmlHttp.status == 200) {
	    		clearTimeout(this.timer);
	    		var json = commonTools.trim(this.xmlHttp.responseText);
	    		if (typeof(json) == "undefined" || json == "") {
		        	setting.error(json);
		        } else {
		        	setting.callback(eval("("+json+")"));
		        }
	    	} else {
	    		clearTimeout(this.timer);
        		setting.error("timeOut");
	    	}
	    }
	},
	createXMLHttpRequest : function() {
	    var xmlh = null;
	    if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
	        xmlh = new XMLHttpRequest();
	    } else if (window.ActiveXObject) {
	        xmlh = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
	    }
	    return xmlh;
	}
};

function getAuthenticationAttr(name) {
    if ((typeof Authentication) != "undefined") {
        return Authentication.CTCGetConfig(name);
    } else {
        return "---";
    }
}

function jsonpData(setting){
	var callbackName = ('jsonp_' + Math.random()).replace(".", "");
	var userId = getAuthenticationAttr("UserID");//从机顶盒信息中获取userId
    var script = document.createElement('script');
    var query = [];
    setting.url = setting.url.indexOf("http://") == 0 ? setting.url : "http://115.233.200.59:58007/epg/"+setting.url;
    setting.data = setting.data || {};
    setting.callback = setting.callback || function(){};
    setting.error = setting.error || setting.callback;
    setting.duration = setting.duration || 1000*2;
    setting.data['callback'] = callbackName;
    setting.data['userId'] = encodeURIComponent(userId);//往参数数组中添加userId
    for(var key in setting.data){
        query.push(key + '=' + encodeURIComponent(setting.data[key]));
    }

    window[callbackName] = function (json) {
    	clearTimeout(script.timer);
        document.head.removeChild(script);
        window[callbackName] = null;
        if (typeof(json) == "undefined") {
        	setting.error(json);
        } else if (setting.url.indexOf("http://115.233.200.59:58007/epg/") != -1 && json.status != 200) {//成思VIS数据接口状态!=200进入错误函数
        	setting.error(json);
        } else if (setting.url.indexOf(userDamon) != -1 && json.status != 200) {//用户管理系统接口状态!=200进入错误函数
        	setting.error(json);
        } else {
        	setting.callback(json);
        }
    };

    script.timer = setTimeout(function() {
    	window[callbackName] = null;
    	document.head.removeChild(script);
		setting.error("timeOut");
	}, setting.duration);
    
    script.id = "jsonPScript";
	if(setting.url.indexOf("?")!=-1){
    	script.src = setting.url + '&' + query.join('&');
	}else{
		script.src = setting.url + '?' + query.join('&');
	}
    document.head.appendChild(script);
}

var smsCommon = {
    loginCount : 0,
	userToken : "",
    loginParams : {},
	RESULT_CODE : {
        "CODE_200" : 200,	// 接口调用成功
		"CODE_400" : 400,	// 请求参数有误或请求无法被服务器理解
		"CODE_403" : 403	// 客户端凭证不可信或者无效
	},
    init : function (params) {
        this.loginParams = params;
        this.loginParams.stbType = Authentication.CTCGetConfig('STBType');
    },
    invalidToken : function (status) {
        if (typeof(status) == "undefined" || status == null || status == "") {
            return false;
        }

        if (status == smsCommon.RESULT_CODE.CODE_400 || status == smsCommon.RESULT_CODE.CODE_403) {
            return true;
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    },
    getToken : function() {
        /** 为解决首页用户登录成功后马上调用getCookie("userToken")获取不到token的情况，通过userToken进行保存，获取时优先返回此token */
    	if (smsCommon.userToken != "" && smsCommon.userToken != commonCookie.getCookie("userToken")) {
    		commonCookie.setCookie("userToken", smsCommon.userToken);
    		return smsCommon.userToken;
		}
        return commonCookie.getCookie("userToken");
    },
    userLogin : function (setting) {
        if (smsCommon.loginCount > 1) {
            smsCommon.loginCount = 0; // 重置
            if (typeof(setting.nextCbFun) == "function") {
                setting.nextCbFun(setting.nextCbFunParams);
            }
            return;
        }

        jsonpData({
            url: userDamon+'auth/epgLogin',
            data: this.loginParams,
            callback: function(data){
                smsCommon.loginCount += 1;
                if(data.status == 200){
                    var token = data.data.token;
                    smsCommon.userToken = token;
                    commonCookie.setCookie("userToken", token);
                    if (typeof(setting.cbFun) == "function") setting.cbFun(setting.cbFunParams);
                } else {
                    if (typeof(setting.nextCbFun) == "function") setting.nextCbFun(setting.nextCbFunParams);
                }
            }
        });
    }
};

var adModule = {
	adDamon : "http://115.233.200.162:8082/",	//test： 155:9010 ， product：162:8082    146:9020
	adUrl : '',								//广告具体地址
	adFlag : false,							//广告开关
	adView : false,							//广告显示标识，适用于广告在展示中
	adInterval : 0,							//广告倒计时周期方法
	adST : 0,								//延时方法
	adTime : 0,								//广告倒计时
	adParams : {},							//广告基础参数
	adExposureData : {},					//广告曝光数据列表
	adExposureTimer : 0,					//广告曝光定时
	adInit : function(_key, _userid, _areaCode, _epgGroup, _mediaCode, _mediaTag, _channelCode){
		if(_key == undefined) _key = '';
		if(_userid == undefined) _userid = '';
		if(_areaCode == undefined) _areaCode = '';
		if(_epgGroup == undefined) _epgGroup = '';
		if(_mediaCode == undefined) _mediaCode = '';
		if(_channelCode == undefined) _channelCode = '';
		if(_mediaTag == undefined) _mediaTag = '';
		this.adParams.secretKey = _key;
		this.adParams.iptvAccount = _userid;
		this.adParams.areaCode = _areaCode;
		this.adParams.epgGroup = _epgGroup;
		this.adParams.mediaCode = _mediaCode;
		this.adParams.mediaTag = _mediaTag;
		this.adParams.channelCode = _channelCode;
	},
	adGet : function(_posCode, callBackFunction){
		if(!adModule.adFlag && typeof(callBackFunction) == 'function') callBackFunction();
		if(!adModule.adFlag || adModule.adView || _posCode == '') return true;
		
		this.adUrl = this.adDamon + 'adms/epg/ad/check';
		if(_posCode.indexOf(',') != -1) this.adUrl = this.adDamon + 'adms/epg/ad/list/check';
		jsonpData({
            url: this.adUrl,
            data: {adPosCode:_posCode, secretKey:this.adParams.secretKey, iptvAccount:this.adParams.iptvAccount, channelCode:this.adParams.channelCode, mediaCode:this.adParams.mediaCode, tag:this.adParams.mediaTag, areaCode:this.adParams.areaCode, epgGroup:this.adParams.epgGroup, stbType:Authentication.CTCGetConfig('STBType')},
            callback: function(data){
				if (_posCode.indexOf(',') != -1) {//首页推荐查询多个广告位专用
					var _posCodeList = _posCode.split(",");
					for (var i = 0; i < _posCodeList.length; i++) {
						if (data.data[_posCodeList[i]].flag) {
							adModule.adExposureData[_posCodeList[i]] = {
								"exposure":true,
								"impId":data.data[_posCodeList[i]].reqId,
								"materialId":data.data[_posCodeList[i]].ads[0].materialCode,
								"event":data.data[_posCodeList[i]].ads[0].feedbackEvent
							};
						}
					}
				} else if (data.data.flag) {
					var feedbackEventList = [];
					if (data.data.ads[0].feedbackEvent.indexOf(",") != -1) {
						feedbackEventList = data.data.ads[0].feedbackEvent.split(",");
					} else {
						feedbackEventList = [data.data.ads[0].feedbackEvent];
					}
					adModule.adExposureData[_posCode] = {"exposure":true,list:[]};
					for (var i = 0; i < feedbackEventList.length; i++) {
						adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list[i] = {
							"exposure":true,
							"impId":data.data.reqId,
							"materialId":data.data.ads[0].materialCode,
							"event":feedbackEventList[i]
						};
					}
				}
            	if(data.status == '200' && data.data.flag && _posCode.indexOf(',') == -1) {
					for (var i = 0; i < data.data.ads.length; i++) {
						adModule.adTime += parseInt(data.data.ads[i].duration,10);
					}
				}
            	callBackFunction(data);
            },
            error : function(data) {
            	callBackFunction(data);
            }
		});
	},
	adNextSchedule : function(_posCode, callBackFunction){
		if(!adModule.adFlag && typeof(callBackFunction) == 'function') callBackFunction();
		if(!adModule.adFlag || adModule.adView || _posCode == '') return true;
		jsonpData({
            url : adModule.adDamon + "adms/epg/ad/getNextScheduleTime",
            data : {adPosCode:paramsAll.adCode, secretKey:this.adParams.secretKey, areaCode:this.adParams.areaCode, iptvAccount:this.adParams.iptvAccount},
            callback : function(data) {
            	callBackFunction(data);
            },
            error : function(data) {
            	callBackFunction(data);
            }
        });
	},
	adExposure : function(_posCode, type, callBackFunction) {
		if (type == 0 && !adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].exposure) {
			if (typeof(callBackFunction) == 'function') callBackFunction();
			return false;
		}
		
		var exposureJson = {}, exposureIndex = 0, setTimeStr = 0;
		if (adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list.length <= 1) {
			exposureJson = adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list[0];
		} else {
			for (var i = 0; i < adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list.length; i++) {
				exposureJson = adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list[i];
				if (exposureJson.exposure) {
					exposureIndex = i;
					if (adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list.length > (i+1)) {
						var nowIndex = adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list[i].event;
						var nextIndex = adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list[i+1].event;
						if (nextIndex <= 4) {
							setTimeStr = Math.round(adModule.adTime * 0.25 * nextIndex) - Math.round(adModule.adTime * 0.25 * nowIndex);
						}
					}
					break;
				}
			}
		}

		clearTimeout(adModule.adExposureTimer);
		if (setTimeStr > 0) {
			adModule.adExposureTimer = setTimeout(function() {
				adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].exposure = true;
				adModule.adExposure(_posCode, type);
			},1000*setTimeStr);
		}
		
		jsonpData({
            url : adModule.adDamon + "adms/feedback/collect",
            data : {
				secretKey : this.adParams.secretKey,
				areaCode : this.adParams.areaCode,
				iptvAccount : this.adParams.iptvAccount,
				type : type,
				impId : exposureJson.impId,
				materialId : exposureJson.materialId,
				event : exposureJson.event,
			},
            callback : function(data) {
				adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].exposure = false;
				adModule.adExposureData[_posCode].list[exposureIndex].exposure = false;
            	callBackFunction(data);
            },
            error : function(data) {
            	callBackFunction(data);
            }
        });
	},
	adHide : function(){
		if ($('adDiv')) commonTools.removeElement('adDiv');
		if ($('adCountdown')) commonTools.removeElement('adCountdown');
		clearInterval(adModule.adInterval);
		adModule.adView = false;
	}
};
